Title: Transiting Exoplanet Monitoring Project (TEMP). VI. The Homogeneous
    Refinement of System Parameters for 39 Transiting Hot Jupiters with 127
    New Light Curves 
Authors: Wang X.-Y., Wang Y.-H., Wang S., Wu Z.-Y., Rice M., Zhou X.,
    Hinse T.C., Liu H.-G., Ma B., Peng X., Zhang H., Yu C., Zhou J.-L., 
    Laughlin G.
Table: System Parameters for TEMP Targets obtained in This Study are Compared 
    with Literature Values
================================================================================
Byte-by-byte Description of file: datafile4.txt
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   Bytes Format Units   Label   Explanations
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
   1- 10 A10    ---     Planet  Planet Name
  12- 12 A1     ---     SP      [SP] Parameter, Stellar or Planetary
  14- 31 A18    ---     Param   Parameter (1)
  33- 49 F17.9  ---     Value   Value derived in this work
  51- 64 F14.9  ---   E_Value   Upper uncertainty on Value
  66- 79 F14.9  ---   e_Value   Lower uncertainty on Value
  81-104 F24.19 ---     Lit     ?="" Literature value
 106-130 F25.20 ---   E_Lit     ?="" Upper uncertainty on Lit
 132-156 F25.20 ---   e_Lit     ?="" Lower uncertainty on Lit
 158-162 F5.2   ---     sigma   ?="" Agreement, {sigma}
 164-182 A19    ---   r_Lit     Bibcode for literature value
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Note (1): Parameter explanations -- 
    M_*                = Mass, solar units (Stellar Parameter);
    R_*                = Radius, solar units, (Stellar Parameter);
    L_*                = Luminosity, solar units (Stellar Parameter);
    \rho_*             = Density ({rho}), g/cm3 (Stellar Parameter);
    \log{g}            = Log, surface gravity, cm/s2 (Stellar Parameter);
    T_{\rmeff}         = Effective temperature, K (Stellar Parameter);
    [{\rmFe/H}]        = Metallicity (Stellar Parameter);
    Age                = Age, Gyr (Stellar Parameter);
    P                  = Period, days (Planetary Parameter);
    R_P                = Radius, Jovian units (Planetary Parameter);
    M_P                = Mass, Jovian units (Planetary Parameter);
    T_C                = Time of conjunction (BJD at TDB) (Planetary Parameter);
    T_0                = Optimal conjunction Time (BJD at TDB ) (Planetary Parameter);
    a                  = Semi-major axis, au (Planetary Parameter);
    i                  = inclination, degrees (Planetary Parameter);
    e                  = eccentricity (Planetary Parameter);
    \omega_*           = Argument of Periastron, degrees (Planetary Parameter);
    T_{eq}             = Equilibrium temperature, K (Planetary Parameter);
    \tau_{\rmcirc}     = Tidal circularization timescale, Gyr (Planetary Parameter);
    K                  = RV semi-amplitude, m/s (Planetary Parameter);
    \log{K}            = Log of RV semi-amplitude (Planetary Parameter);
    R_P/R_*            = Radius of planet in stellar radii (Planetary Parameter);
    a/R_*              = Semi-major axis in stellar radii (Planetary Parameter);
    \delta             = Transit depth, fraction (Planetary Parameter);
    Depth              = Flux decrement at mid transit (Planetary Parameter);
    \tau               = Ingress/egress transit duration, days (Planetary Parameter);
    T_{14}             = Total transit duration, days (Planetary Parameter);
    T_{FWHM}           = FWHM transit duration, days (Planetary Parameter);
    b                  = Transit Impact parameter (Planetary Parameter);
    b_S                = Eclipse impact parameter (Planetary Parameter);
    \tau_S             = Ingress/egress eclipse duration, days (Planetary Parameter);
    T_{S_14}           = Total eclipse duration, days (Planetary Parameter);
    T_{S_FWHM}         = FWHM eclipse duration, days (Planetary Parameter);
    \delta_{S_3.6\mum} = Blackbody eclipse depth at 3.6um, ppm (Planetary Parameter);
    \delta_{S_4.5\mum} = Blackbody eclipse depth at 4.5um, ppm (Planetary Parameter);
    \rho_P             = Density, g/cm3 (Planetary Parameter);
    logg_P             = log, surface gravity, cm/s2 (Planetary Parameter);
    \Theta             = Safronov Number (Planetary Parameter);
    \fave              = Incident Flux, 10+9 erg/s/cm2 (Planetary Parameter);
    T_P                = Time of periastron, BJD at TDB (Planetary Parameter);
    T_S                = Time of eclipse, BJD at TDB (Planetary Parameter);
    T_A                = Time of ascending node, BJD at TDB (Planetary Parameter);
    T_D                = Time of descending node, BJD at TDB (Planetary Parameter);
    e\cos{\omega_*}    = eccentricity * cos({omega}*) (Planetary Parameter);
    e\sin{\omega_*}    = eccentricity * sin({omega}*) (Planetary Parameter);
    M_P\sini           = Minimum mass, Jovian units (Planetary Parameter);
    M_P/M_*            = Mass ratio (Planetary Parameter);
    d/R_*              = Separation at mid transit  (Planetary Parameter);
    P_T                = A priori non-grazing transit probability (Planetary Parameter);
    P_{T_G}            = A priori transit probability (Planetary Parameter);
    P_S                = A priori non-grazing eclipse probability (Planetary Parameter);
    P_{S_G}            = A priori eclipse probability (Planetary Parameter).
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
